The Embassy of Pakistan to Sweden and Finland is initiating a LinkedIn group. 

This group is open to all professionals, students, researchers and academics of Pakistani origin/heritage in Sweden and Finland as well as those who have studied or worked in these countries in the past .

The purpose is to establish a network to exchange ideas on relevant issues important for development of Pakistan and relations between Pakistan and Sweden/Finland.

Through this group we hope that younger students and entrants can benefit from the experiences and mentoring of those who have more experience.

We also hope it will improve the communication between the Embassy and our community and result in ideas to further develop Pakistanâ€™s relations in various fields with these countries.

You can join the group through the link mentioned below:

7/28/21, 12:48 PM - +92 322 9929947: Dear Faisal Waheed Khan

 

Thank you for your message. The Finnish Consular Act as well as the Decree no 613/2015  of the President of the Republic of Finland defines the operating areas of the Finnish embassies. The immigration matters of Pakistani citizens fall under the jurisdiction of the Embassy of Finland in Abu Dhabi, UAE. Therefore it is unfortunately not possible to process your application in any other country. Please be in direct contact with the Embassy in UAE in relation to your application process. Their contacts are following: https://finlandabroad.fi/web/are/contact

 

Further, any individual solutions are unfortunately not possible such as making the interview at another Embassy or in Finland upon arrival. Covid-19 pandemic does not constitute grounds for making exception to this rule. It is worth remembering that any decisions made will have to be based on principle of equality, i.e all the applicants should have the same rights. The Embassies are prepared to serve in their respective host countries in its languages, having all the necessary knowledge and expertise on the  documentation and other relevant matters which are important to handle the applications. Therefore, certain embassies are qualified to act to the best of the applicant, but only in their own territory.

 

We are aware that the restrictions have caused a very difficult and disappointing situation for You, as well as many other people and travelers stranded in difficult situations.

 

The Corona virus pandemic has required very difficult decisions that have also harmful impacts.  We hope that the situation will be normalized soon.

 

 

With kind regards

 

Visa Unit

Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Finland

Helsinki

Your Excellency,

I hope this email finds you well.

As discussed with your excellency over the past few online meetings regarding the student visas issue, I would like to bring to your notice that the registration deadlines of most of the Finnish Universities are very near. Yours Sincerely,
Ausaf Ali Khan (On behalf of Pakistani Students)

8/4/21, 11:23 AM - +92 332 3255525: Dear All Airlines / Private Operators

We write with reference to the above subject.

Please be informed that, effective from Thursday 5th August 2021 00:01 hrs., the following amended conditions will be applicable for the operation of international air services.

Decision â€“ 1: Entering UAE

With regard to the countries listed below, the restrictions imposed previously will be amended for the categories referred to in Clause 1 below and will be granted permission to ENTER United Arab Emirates (UAE), subject to their compliance of the conditions set out in Clause 2 below.

The applicable Countries:
1.	The Republic of India
2.	The Federal Democratic Republic of Nepal   
3.	Federal Republic of Nigeria
4.	The Islamic Republic of Pakistan
5.	The Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
6.	The Republic of Uganda
1.           The removal of restrictions will be applicable to the following categories: 

1.                  A holder of valid UAE resident visa, who has obtained the required vaccination doses in the UAE and completed fourteen (14) days after the 2nd dose and holds a vaccination card issued from a medical institution in the UAE, including the vaccine certificate available in the smart application(s) of Government Medical entities in the UAE;
2.                  Members of the medical force/staff including Doctors, Nurses and Medical Technicians (Whether Vaccinated or not Vaccinated);
3.                  Staff/Employees of Educational Sector, including Professors and Teachers, those who teaches at Universities, Colleges, Schools and Institutions in the UAE (Whether Vaccinated or not vaccinated);
4.                  Students who are currently studying in the UAE (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
5.                  Those who are holding a valid visa, on humanitarian grounds and/or cases (i.e. family reunion) (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
6.                  Employees/Staff of Local and Federal Government entities (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
7.                  Those who undergo medical treatments in UAE (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);

2.           All passengers who are exempted as provided in Clause 1 above,  shall ensure that the following preventive measures are compiled by them:-

(a)         Hold a VALID Negative Covid-19 Test certificate that is issued within the valid time frame, namely, (48) hours from the time of collecting the sample. Issued from approved health service,  which use QR code System;
(b)         Rapid test conducted before boarding the aircraft from the departure country;
(c)          Undergo a PCR test at the arriving airport;

3.           Methods of implementation:

a)                  The passenger shall submit a request through the website of the General Directorate of Residency and Foreigners Affairs, for the necessary approval;
The Website: https://smart.gdrfad.gov.ae/homepage.aspx 
b)                  A holder of valid UAE resident visa, who has obtained the required vaccination doses in the UAE and completed fourteen (14) days after the 2nd dose, shall submit the vaccination certificate/card through the website of the General Directorate of Residency and Foreigners Affairs, through https://smart.gdrfad.gov.ae/homepage.aspx
c)                  The airlines shall ensure and/or verify the authenticity of the above requirement(s) prior to the passenger(s) boarding the aircraft and shall not accept any passenger(s) who does not fulfill the aforesaid condition(s) and/or requirements; 
If the airline carries any passenger(s) who fails to meet the aforesaid requirements, the airline will be held responsible to return such passenger to the point of embarkation and also any other matters that may arise therefrom.

Decision -2: Transiting through UAE

With regard to the countries listed below, the restrictions imposed previously will be amended for the categories referred to in Clause 1 below and will be granted permission to TRANSIT through United Arab Emirates, subject to their compliance of the  conditions set out in Clause 1 below.
1.	The People's Republic of Bangladesh
2.	The Democratic Republic of the Congo
3.	The Republic of India
4.	the Republic of Liberia
5.	the Republic of Namibia
6.	The Federal Democratic Republic of Nepal   
7.	Federal Republic of Nigeria
8.	The Islamic Republic of Pakistan
9.	the Republic of Sierra Leone
10.	The Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
11.	Republic of South Africa
12.	The Republic of Uganda
13.	Socialist Republic of Vietnam
14.	The Republic of Zambia

1.           All passengers who are traveling from Countries exempted as provided in Decision 2 above and transiting through UAE, shall ensure that the following preventive measures are compiled by them:
                                                                           
a)                  Obtain necessary entry permission/approval from Country of the final destination;
b)                  Hold a VALID Negative Covid-19 Test certificate that is issued within the valid time frame, namely, (72) hours from the time of collecting the sample. Issued from approved health service,  which use QR code System;
c)                  The airlines shall ensure and/or verify the authenticity of the above requirement(s) prior to the passenger(s) boarding the aircraft and shall not accept any passenger(s) who does not fulfill the aforesaid condition(s) and/or requirements; 
If the airline carries any passenger(s) who fails to meet the aforesaid requirements, the airline will be held responsible to return such passenger to the point of embarkation and also any other matters that may arise therefrom.

Air Carriers that fail and/or neglect to comply with the measures set out in this decision will be subject to the fines and measures stipulated in Clause 37 of Schedule No. (7) of the Executive Council Resolution No. (4) of 2017 Approving Fees and Fines of the Dubai Civil Aviation Authority, considering that adherence to the provisions of DCAA Circular No. (1) of 2021, is strictly required for Air Carriers to continue practicing air transport activity arriving to or transiting through Dubai.

8/5/21, 10:31 AM - +92 305 5252002: Dear All Airlines / Private Operators
 
We write with reference to the above subject.
 
Please be informed that, effective from Thursday 5th August 2021 00:01 hrs., the following amended conditions will be applicable for the operation of international air services.
 
Decision â€“ 1: Entering UAE
 
With regard to the countries listed below, the restrictions imposed previously will be amended for the categories referred to in Clause 1 below and will be granted permission to ENTER United Arab Emirates (UAE), subject to their compliance of the conditions set out in Clause 2 below.
 
The applicable Countries:
The Republic of India
The Federal Democratic Republic of Nepal   
Federal Republic of Nigeria
The Islamic Republic of Pakistan
The Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
The Republic of Uganda
1.           The removal of restrictions will be applicable to the following categories:
 
1.                  A holder of valid UAE resident visa, who has obtained the required vaccination doses in the UAE and completed fourteen (14) days after the 2nd dose and holds a vaccination card issued from a medical institution in the UAE, including the vaccine certificate available in the smart application(s) of Government Medical entities in the UAE;
2.                  Members of the medical force/staff including Doctors, Nurses and Medical Technicians (Whether Vaccinated or not Vaccinated);
3.                  Staff/Employees of Educational Sector, including Professors and Teachers, those who teaches at Universities, Colleges, Schools and Institutions in the UAE (Whether Vaccinated or not vaccinated);
4.                  Students who are currently studying in the UAE (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
5.                  Those who are holding a valid visa, on humanitarian grounds and/or cases (i.e. family reunion) (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
6.                  Employees/Staff of Local and Federal Government entities (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
7.                  Those who undergo medical treatments in UAE (Whether vaccinated or not vaccinated);
 
2.           All passengers who are exempted as provided in Clause 1 above,  shall ensure that the following preventive measures are compiled by them:-
 
(a)         Hold a VALID Negative Covid-19 Test certificate that is issued within the valid time frame, namely, (48) hours from the time of collecting the sample. Issued from approved health service,  which use QR code System;
(b)         Rapid test conducted before boarding the aircraft from the departure country;
(c)          Undergo a PCR test at the arriving airport;
 
3.           Methods of implementation:
 
a)                  The passenger shall submit a request through the website of the General Directorate of Residency and Foreigners Affairs, for the necessary approval;
The Website: https://smart.gdrfad.gov.ae/homepage.aspx
b)                  A holder of valid UAE resident visa, who has obtained the required vaccination doses in the UAE and completed fourteen (14) days after the 2nd dose, shall submit the vaccination certificate/card through the website of the General Directorate of Residency and Foreigners Affairs, through https://smart.gdrfad.gov.ae/homepage.aspx
c)                  The airlines shall ensure and/or verify the authenticity of the above requirement(s) prior to the passenger(s) boarding the aircraft and shall not accept any passenger(s) who does not fulfill the aforesaid condition(s) and/or requirements;
If the airline carries any passenger(s) who fails to meet the aforesaid requirements, the airline will be held responsible to return such passenger to the point of embarkation and also any other matters that may arise therefrom.
 
Decision -2: Transiting through UAE
 
With regard to the countries listed below, the restrictions imposed previously will be amended for the categories referred to in Clause 1 below and will be granted permission to TRANSIT through United Arab Emirates, subject to their compliance of the  conditions set out in Clause 1 below.
The People's Republic of Bangladesh
The Democratic Republic of the Congo
The Republic of India
the Republic of Liberia
the Republic of Namibia
The Federal Democratic Republic of Nepal   
Federal Republic of Nigeria
The Islamic Republic of Pakistan
the Republic of Sierra Leone
The Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
Republic of South Africa
The Republic of Uganda
Socialist Republic of Vietnam
The Republic of Zambia
 
1.           All passengers who are traveling from Countries exempted as provided in Decision 2 above and transiting through UAE, shall ensure that the following preventive measures are compiled by them:
                                                                          
a)                  Obtain necessary entry permission/approval from Country of the final destination;
b)                  Hold a VALID Negative Covid-19 Test certificate that is issued within the valid time frame, namely, (72) hours from the time of collecting the sample. Issued from approved health service,  which use QR code System;
c)                  The airlines shall ensure and/or verify the authenticity of the above requirement(s) prior to the passenger(s) boarding the aircraft and shall not accept any passenger(s) who does not fulfill the aforesaid condition(s) and/or requirements;
If the airline carries any passenger(s) who fails to meet the aforesaid requirements, the airline will be held responsible to return such passenger to the point of embarkation and also any other matters that may arise therefrom.
 
Air Carriers that fail and/or neglect to comply with the measures set out in this decision will be subject to the fines and measures stipulated in Clause 37 of Schedule No. (7) of the Executive Council Resolution No. (4) of 2017 Approving Fees and Fines of the Dubai Civil Aviation Authority, considering that adherence to the provisions of DCAA Circular No. (1) of 2021, is strictly required for Air Carriers to continue practicing air transport activity arriving to or transiting through Dubai.
 
Your continuous support to curtail the spread of COVID-19 (Coronavirus SARS Cov-2), is greatly appreciated!
 
Best Regards,
 
Air Transport Operations
Dubai Civil Aviation Authority

8/6/21, 11:02 AM - +92 333 2698416: Travelers to UAE
Step 1: Vaccinated from Pakistan: Upload your vaccine certificate and request to upload records in AlHosn App. For Example: Nadra Certificate in Pakistan. https://www.dha.gov.ae/en/covid19/pages/mrneid.aspx 
Step 2: Install AlHosn App.
Step 3: Enter your Emirates ID and generate the certificate.
Step 4: Go to GDFRA (Dubai Visa Holders) https://smart.gdrfad.gov.ae/.../ReturnPermitServiceForm.aspx on the step 3 upload vaccination certificate, passport, visa and emirates id, you will get approval on the email in a day.
Step 5: At least 24 hours before, apply for ICA approval https://smartservices.ica.gov.ae/.../guest/index.html...
Step 6: Must do Anti Rapid Test from the following Approved Labs ONLY 4 hours before flight time 
Chughtai Lab
Excel Labs
Islamabad Diagnostic Center (IDC)
Essa Lab
Shaukat Khanum
 Must Report Airport 3 hours Plus before the flight time to avoid any issues 
** Fly Dubai only Boarding GDFRA Dubai Visa Passengers , Not lifting ICA ( Abu Dhabi / Sharjah Visa Holders ) 
As per news, Pakistan government start the facility for Covid Rapid Test from 9th August.

8/8/21, 3:08 PM - +92 333 9153804: Dear Sir/Madam,

 

Thank you for your message. We fully understand that this unfortunate situation may have major implications on lives of individuals. Unfortunately, there is little Embassy can do to mitigate the COVID situation, the COVID restrictions and their implications on residence permit applicants.


The immigration matters of Pakistani citizens fall under the jurisdiction of the Embassy of Finland in Abu Dhabi. If you want to apply for the residence permit in other country you need to send email to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Helsinki to Residence permit and passport unit KPA-20@formin.fi

 

The Ministry needs the following information:

 

-          Which applicants (names of applicants and birth day, passport details, nationality)

-          Personal details of the family member (name and date of birth and customer number)

-          Description of the situation

Â·       What have the customer done to made it to the actual point of service (in this case Abu Dhabi)

Â·       Why is it impossible to get to the service point and is there a reason that is not the applicants reason.

Â·       To which service point (Finnish Embassy) applicant would like to go.

 

Unfortunately it is mandatory to visit Embassy of Finland in order to submit your residence permit. Therefore, it is not possible to submit biometrics in Pakistan. 


 

Best Regards,

 

Janni Nurmi

 

Consular Services

Hello
From the tuition fee point of view:
Â·If you complete any studies during Autumn semester (online or on campus) you are
required to pay the tuition fee for the whole Autumn Semester.
Â·If you register as absent for the Spring semester, no fees are charged for Spring
semester.This part of payment can be postponed for next year or refunded if you
decide to give up your study place.
Â·If you do NOT complete any studies and postpone the start for COVID-reasons,
your paid tuition fee will be also postponed for next year.
Â·If you do NOT complete any studies and decide to cancel, your paid tuition fee will
be fully refunded.
From the scholarship point of view:
Â·If you are present for the whole year. A total of 60 credits is needed from the first
academic year, to gain a 50% scholarship for the second year.
Â·lf you only study during the autumn semester and are not able to arrive for Spring
semester for COVID-reasons (delay with RP-process), 30 credits from Autumn
semester is needed for the second year scholarship.
Best regards,
LUT University
Scholarship team/Niina M.

8/19/21, 8:35 PM - +92 308 7512101: Guys! I know that it's out of context at this moment but I wanted to advise the PhD students here. It's is better to start working on your research with your current supervisors. 1. Ask them to share some literature with you. 2. Discuss research ideas with them. 3. Ask them if any conference is coming in the near future. 4. Start writing a research paper as soon as you can. This approach will help you a lot with the start of your PhD studies. It can also be counted in your PhD Thesis. And looking at your progress, your supervisors might help you go through this difficult time of Visa processing by allowing you to have a delayed start because you are already working remotely if not officially. I hope this might help you guys. Best of luck.

8/21/21, 1:59 PM - +92 333 2698416: Reply of Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Finland:

"Thankyou for your message. The Finnish Consular Act as well as the Decree no 613/2015  of the President of the Republic of Finland defines the operating areas of the Finnish embassies. The immigration matters of Pakistani citizens fall under the jurisdiction of the Embassy of Finland in Abu Dhabi, UAE. Therefore it is unfortunately not possible to process your application in any other country. Please be in direct contact with the Embassy in UAE in relation to your application process. Their contacts are following: https://finlandabroad.fi/web/are/contact

Further, any individual solutions are unfortunately not possible such as making the interview at another Embassy or in Finland upon arrival. Covid-19 pandemic does not constitute grounds for making exception to this rule. It is worth remembering that any decisions made will have to be based on principle of equality, i.e all the applicants should have the same rights. The Embassies are prepared to serve in their respective host countries in its languages, having all the necessary knowledge and expertise on the  documentation and other relevant matters which are important to handle the applications. Therefore, certain embassies are qualified to act to the best of the applicant, but only in their own territory.

We are aware that the restrictions have caused a very difficult and disappointing situation for You, as well as many other people and travelers stranded in difficult situations.

The Corona virus pandemic has required very difficult decisions that have also harmful impacts.  We hope that the situation will be normalized soon.

With kind regards

Visa Unit

Ministry for Foreign Affairs of Finland

Helsinki"

Hello
From the tuition fee point of view:
Â·If you complete any studies during Autumn semester (online or on campus) you are
required to pay the tuition fee for the whole Autumn Semester.
Â·If you register as absent for the Spring semester, no fees are charged for Spring
semester.This part of payment can be postponed for next year or refunded if you
decide to give up your study place.
Â·If you do NOT complete any studies and postpone the start for COVID-reasons,
your paid tuition fee will be also postponed for next year.
Â·If you do NOT complete any studies and decide to cancel, your paid tuition fee will
be fully refunded.
From the scholarship point of view:
Â·If you are present for the whole year. A total of 60 credits is needed from the first
academic year, to gain a 50% scholarship for the second year.
Â·lf you only study during the autumn semester and are not able to arrive for Spring
semester for COVID-reasons (delay with RP-process), 30 credits from Autumn
semester is needed for the second year scholarship.
Best regards,
LUT University
Scholarship team/Niina M.

Requirements for all passengers arriving in Dubai

All passengers travelling to Dubai from any point of origin (GCC countries included) must hold a negative COVIDâ€‘19 RTâ€‘PCR test certificate for a test taken no more than 72 hours before departure, except for travel from Afghanistan, Bangladesh, Indonesia, India, Pakistan and Sri Lanka (for which specific requirements are stated below). Please see the requirements for travel from India below.

The certificate must be a Reverse Transcriptionâ€‘Polymerase Chain Reaction (RTâ€‘PCR) test. Other test certificates including antibody tests, NHS COVID Test certificates, Rapid PCR tests and home testing kits are not accepted in Dubai. Travellers must bring an official, digital or printed certificate in English or Arabic to check in â€“ SMS certificates are not accepted. PCR certificates in other languages are acceptable if they can be validated at the originating station. Digital COVIDâ€‘19 certificates are accepted upon arrival at Dubai International airport verification points.

COVIDâ€‘19 RTâ€‘PCR test certificates must be issued by an authorised facility in the passenger's departure country. Certificates that have already been presented for travel to another destination can't be used for reâ€‘entry even if they are still within the validity period.

For passengers arriving from the following countries, it is mandatory that the COVIDâ€‘19 PCR report includes a QR code linked to the original report for verification purposes. 8/31/21, 7:06 PM - +92 322 9929947: Travelling to Dubai - rules as of 30 August 2021
Rules for Dubai residence visa holders
All UAE residents can travel to Dubai without an approval from GDRFA or ICA except those travelling from:
 
Bangladesh
India
Indonesia
Nigeria
Pakistan
Sri Lanka
South Africa
Uganda
Vietnam
Zambia.
 

However, approval is not needed for those coming from one of the 10 countries mentioned above and those who have one of the following:

a newly issued residence or employment visa
a short stay or long stay visa
a visit visa or
a visa on arrival.
 

Requirements for passengers from these countries:

Passengers arriving from the countries above must present a printed negative result of a COVIDâ€‘19 PCR test issued within 48 hours of the time the sample was collected at an approved health facility (PDF, 100 KB). The certificate must contain a QR code.
Passengers must also present a negative result (with a QR code) of a rapid PCR test conducted at the departure airport within six hours before departure.
 

Passengers travelling from other countries must present a printed negative result of a COVIDâ€‘19 RT PCR test done no more than 72 hours before departure.

 

*Certificates that have already been presented for travel to another destination can't be used for reâ€‘entry even if they are still within the validity period.

 

Exemptions for the COVIDâ€‘19 PCR test
The following people are exempt from getting a COVID-19 test at the departure airport, but have to undergo a test on arrival in Dubai:

all UAE nationals returning to Dubai from any country
nonâ€‘UAE nationals accompanying a firstâ€‘degree UAE national family member
domestic workers accompanying a UAE national sponsor
children below 12 years old
passengers with moderate to severe disabilities.
 

Test on arrival

All passengers arriving in Dubai from the following countries will be required to take another COVIDâ€‘19 PCR test on arrival at Dubaiâ€™s airports:

Afghanistan, Angola, Argentina, Austria, Azerbaijan, Bahrain, Bangladesh, Bosnia & Herzegovina, Brazil, Cambodia, Chile, Croatia, Cyprus, Djibouti, Egypt, Eritrea, Ethiopia, Georgia, Ghana, Greece, Guinea, Hungary, India, Indonesia, Iran, Iraq, Israel, Ivory Coast, Jordan, Kenya, Kuwait, Kyrgyzstan, Lebanon, Maldives, Malta, Moldova, Montenegro, Morocco, Myanmar, Nepal, Oman, Pakistan, Poland, Philippines, Qatar, Rwanda, Russia, Senegal, Slovakia, Somaliland, Somalia, South Sudan, Sudan, Syria, Tajikistan, Tanzania, Thailand, Tunisia, Turkey, Turkmenistan, Ukraine, Uzbekistan, Zimbabwe.

 

Note:

You must remain in your residence until you receive the test result. If the test result is positive, you will be required to undergo isolation and follow the guidelines of Dubai Health Authority.

9/4/21, 10:21 AM - +971 52 579 6537: Part1
Institutions details 
- institution name
- institution location (city)
- Degree name in which enrolled 
- degree duration 
- contents of degree
- When and why did you select that program?
-Why did you choose that specific university?
- What occupation will you choose after graduating?
- In which occupation or field you will use this degree?

Part 2
Sponsor details
- who is your sponsor?
- your relation with sponsor?
- how much he deposited in your account?
- any large transactions?
- origin date of transactions to your account 
- who paid your tuition fee?

Part 3
Sponsor is salary person
If yes then
- what is job?
- salary after tax


Part 4 sponsor has business or company 
-Are the funds from a business/businesses, if yes state the businesses with their address/email.
-State yearly income of the business/businesses

Part5 Sponsor took loan
-Did your sponsors take a loan?

Part 6 sponsor money from sale of land

Part7 
-Family details.
-Single married 
-Wife name
-Children
-Do you have any dependants?



Part8 
- criminal record
- anyother schengen visa applied
- rejected from schengen visa
- already in Finland 
- ever visited final 
- any family memeber in Finland

9/17/21, 8:30 PM - +92 348 4721872: Part1
Institutions details 
- institution name
- institution location (city)
- Degree name in which enrolled 
- degree duration 
- contents of degree
- When and why did you select that program?
-Why did you choose that specific university?
- What occupation will you choose after graduating?
- In which occupation or field you will use this degree?

Part 2
Sponsor details
- who is your sponsor?
- your relation with sponsor?
- how much he deposited in your account?
- any large transactions?
- origin date of transactions to your account 
- who paid your tuition fee?

Part 3
Sponsor is salary person
If yes then
- what is job?
- salary after tax


Part 4 sponsor has business or company 
-Are the funds from a business/businesses, if yes state the businesses with their address/email.
-State yearly income of the business/businesses

Part5 Sponsor took loan
-Did your sponsors take a loan?

Part 6 sponsor money from sale of land

Part7 
-Family details.
-Single married 
-Wife name
-Children
-Do you have any dependants?



Part8 
- criminal record
- anyother schengen visa applied
- rejected from schengen visa
- already in Finland 
- ever visited final 
- any family memeber in Finland

10/5/21, 2:21 PM - +92 347 6496619: Yesterday, I am done with my appointment at Embassy. Everything went really great. My appointment time was at 8:30. I was there at 8:10 and after 2 minutes they let me in. Soon after that, they gave me a form and 20 minutes to fill that. If you need more time after 20 minutes, then she said you have to ask from us. (Its difficult to write by wearing gloves. So, I took exactly 20 minutes). At 8:30, I was in the interview room. She asked general questions about trip. Now they know that students are coming directly to Abu-Dhabi and they don't need to cross the border. Also, she knows that if you are 35 years old then you will get the single male UAE visa. I don't know how she know that but I kind of  complained that I was unable to get single male UAE visa, rejection rate was high bla bla and she said that you should be 35 years old to get single visa due to polices. So, jo chizain hum discuss karty hain regarding UAE, wo Finnish Embassy waly b janty hi hain.

Then she opened my application and started to check each document one by one which I uploaded. She was really happy that I paid embassy fee (â‚¬350) from my debit card. Again and again she said, "very good, very good". She was also interested to know what are your plans after studies (even answered in paper sheet). Then finger print step and then she explained how this whole process will work. She said, we are the receiver and verifier, we received your application and verified your identity. Now immigration office will issue your card, and will be delivered to us. Keep checking application status from EnterFinland. At the end, she moved my EnterFinland application to in-progress and gave me a diary number. (You can find diary number and case number on EnterFinland website as well when she will move your application to in-progress). It was a hassle free experience.

Last week, one of my friend appeared in Embassy. She took his bank statement and account maintenance certificate. But she didn't keep any document of mine. I even asked do you need any documents? (itni khajal khawari jo hue thi :P ) She said no, everything is good. 

I asked a question. How many students you deal with on a daily basis? She said, depends on the situation but at max we deal with 8 students. 

Lets hope for the best for everyone.
